### ADR-EMG-001

- Kind: `decision`
- Origin: `authored`
- Status: `accepted`
- Title: Generate architecture decision records separately from the main architecture document
- Summary: Model architecture decision records as first-class authored data and generate them into
a separate Architecture Decision Records document. The main architecture document links
to the generated decision records document through a compact decision index.
- Source Refs: SRC-DECISION_DECISIONS_YML_2_5C7E17

### ADR-EMG-002

- Kind: `decision`
- Origin: `authored`
- Status: `accepted`
- Title: Keep architecture decision records model-authored and separate from code links
- Summary: Store architecture decision records as first-class authored model data with required context,
decision, status, date, and consequences. Do not add code-link fields to the ADR model.
- Source Refs: SRC-DECISION_DECISIONS_YML_18_B39E70

## Implementation Paths

### IMPL-EMG-001

- Requirement: `REQ-EMG-001`
- Priority: `medium`
- Goal: While local development mode is active, when model updated event is received, the engineering model go shall validate architecture model before generation run is requested.
  - 1. Confirm requirement intent and acceptance criteria before code changes (`REQ-EMG-001`)
  - 2. Implement or update behavior in functional unit scope and dependent interfaces/flows (`FU-CLI-ORCHESTRATION`)
  - 3. Update code evidence linked to this unit (`CODE-LIBRARY_EXTERNAL_GITHUB_COM_LABETH_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO_F1F304`)
  - 4. Implement or update behavior in functional unit scope and dependent interfaces/flows (`FU-VALIDATION-ENGINE`)
  - 5. Update code evidence linked to this unit (`CODE-LIBRARY_EXTERNAL_GITHUB_COM_LABETH_EARS_LINT_GO_EED44D`)
  - 6. Update or add tests so verification stays passing for this requirement (`VER-INF-TEST-CATALOG_SYSTEMS_TEST-6807D7`)
